                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>পেন্টাইল অ্যাসিটেট&nbsp;</p>

                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">

                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>

                                    </div>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনো রাখো: পাকা কলায় → পেন্টাইল অ্যাসিটেট; পাকা কমলায় → অক্টাইল অ্যাসিটেট; পাকা আনারসে → বিউটাইল বিউটারেট; জেসমিন ফুলে → বেনজাইল অ্যাসিটেট।<br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২৩, পৃষ্ঠা-৩০২]</p>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: বলের দ্বারা কাজ → <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-71-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mn>0</mn><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mo>&amp;#xB0;</mo></mrow><mo>&amp;#x2264;</mo><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mo>&amp;#x3B8;</mo></mrow><mo>&amp;lt;</mo><mn>90</mn><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mo>&amp;#xB0;</mo></mrow></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-737" style="width: 5.699em; top: -2.006em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-738"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-739" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">0</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-740"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-741"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-742" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">°</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-743" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">&lt;</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-748" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">90</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-749"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-750"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-751" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">°</span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; বলের বিরুদ্ধে কাজ → <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-72-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mn>90</mn><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mo>&amp;#xB0;</mo></mrow><mo>&amp;lt;</mo><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mo>&amp;#x3B8;</mo></mrow><mo>&amp;#x2264;</mo><mn>180</mn><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mo>&amp;#xB0;</mo></mrow></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-752" style="width: 6.723em; top: -2.006em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-753"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-754" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">90</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-755"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-756"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-757" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">°</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-758" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; শূন্য কাজ → <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-73-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi>&amp;#x03B8;</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>90</mn><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mo>&amp;#xB0;</mo></mrow></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-767" style="width: 3.322em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.707em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.191em, 1002.54em, 2.174em, -999.998em); top: -2.006em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-768"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-769" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">θ</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-770" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-771" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">90</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-772"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-773"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-774" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">°</span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.01em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.098em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.002em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>θ</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>90</mn><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>°</mo></mrow></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-73">\rm \theta=90°</script></span><br>
[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২৩, পৃষ্ঠা-৩৬৩]</p>

                                        </div>

                                            </div>

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>who</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">

                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">

</label>
                                                
                                            </div>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">

                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>শূন্যস্থানের পর verb এবং পূর্বে ব্যক্তিবাচক sub থাকায় relative pronoun হিসেবে who বসবে। Who যোগে বাক্যটির বাংলা: সততা মহৎ গুণ। যে ব্যক্তি এই অসাধারণ গুণের অধিকারী সে পৃথিবীর সবচেয়ে সুখী মানুষ।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>

                        <div class="row questionBlock">

                            <div class="row question">
                                <div class="col-md-12" style="padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px;">
                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial">
                                            <span>Question 81 </span>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>I have applied for the post of a Lecturer ____ English.</p>

                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="row questionOptions">
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>at</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>of</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>for</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>in</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Subject- এর পূর্বে in preposition টি ব্যবহৃত হয়। In যোগে বাক্যটির বাংলা: আমি ইংরেজি প্রভাষক পদের জন্য আবেদন করেছি।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                        </div>

                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Where was seen by you?</p>
</label>

                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Where was he seen by you?</p>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Wh-word (সাধারণত who ও whom বাদে) দ্বারা শুরু interrogative sentence- এর active voice- কে passive করার নিয়ম: Wh-word টি + tense অনুযায়ী auxiliary verb + object টি subject + মূল verb এর p.p. + by + subject টি object + প্রশ্নবোধক (?) চিহ্ন বসে। সুতরাং নিয়ম অনুসারে সঠিক উত্তর Where was he seen by you?</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Yesterday হলো past indefinite indicator। তাই yesterday থাকলে বাক্যটি past indefinite tense এ হয়। অন্যদিকে die (মারা যাওয়া) শব্দটি passive voice- এ ব্যবহৃত হয় না। সুতরাং একমাত্র সঠিক বাক্য The old man died yesterday।</p>
